		x = 6

				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = AUH
						NOT = {
							tag = AUH
						}
					}
					add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						is_in_faction = no
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_subject_of = AUH
					}
					add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
				}
			}
		
			add_political_power = 50
		}
	}

		icon = GFX_focus_generic_combined_arms
		x = 47
		y = 7
		cost = 10
		prerequisite = { focus = AUH1_endless_advance
                         focus = AUH1_endless_defense }
		completion_reward = {
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = arms_factory
						size > 0
						include_locked = yes
					}
					OR = {
						is_in_home_area = yes
						NOT = {
							owner = {
								any_owned_state = {
									free_building_slots = {
										building = arms_factory
										size > 0
										include_locked = yes
									}
									is_in_home_area = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			add_ideas = { RI_standards }
		}
    }
